(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)


This is previous problem file:

        (door kitchen west open)
    )
    (:goal
        (at corridor)
    )

 (define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
    )

        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
        )

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem exploration-problem)
    (:domain exploration)
    (:objects
        kitchen - location
        corridor - location
        corridor-north-room - location
        corridor-south-room - location
        east-room - location
        west-patio - location
    )
    (:init
        (at kitchen)
        (door kitchen north closed)
        (door kitchen east closed)
        (door kitchen west open)
        (door corridor north closed)
        (door corridor south closed)
        (door corridor east open)
        (door corridor west closed)
        (connected kitchen north corridor-north-room)
        (connected kitchen east east-room)
        (connected kitchen west corridor)
        (connected corridor north corridor-north-room)
        (connected corridor south corridor-south-room)
        (connected corridor east kitchen)
        (connected corridor west west-patio)
    )
    (:goal
        (at west-patio)
    )
)

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)

(define (domain exploration)
    (:requirements :strips)
    (:types location direction state)
    (:constants
        closed open - state
        north east south west - direction
    )
    (:predicates 
        (at ?l - location)
        (door ?l - location ?dir - direction ?s - state)
        (connected ?from - location ?dir - direction ?to - location)
    )
    (:action open-door
        :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?loc1)
            (door ?loc1 ?dir closed)
            (connected ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (door ?loc1 ?dir closed))
            (door ?loc1 ?dir open)
        )
    )
    (:action move
        :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
        :precondition (and 
            (at ?from)
            (door ?from ?dir open)
            (connected ?from ?dir ?to)
        )
        :effect (and 
            (not (at ?from))
            (at ?to)
        )
    )
)
